This leaves several\n   501→ * options for implementing multi-threaded processing of records.\n   502→ *\n   503→ * <h4>1. One Consumer Per Thread</h4>\n   504→ *\n   505→ * A simple option is to give each thread its own consumer instance. Here are the pros and cons of this approach:\n   506→ * <ul>\n   507→ * <li><b>PRO</b>: It is the easiest to implement\n   508→ * <li><b>PRO</b>: It is often the fastest as no inter-thread co-ordination is needed\n   509→ * <li><b>PRO</b>: It makes in-order processing on a per-partition basis very easy to implement (each thread just\n   510→ * processes messages in the order it receives them).\n   511→ * <li><b>CON</b>: More consumers means more TCP connections to the cluster (one per thread). In general Kafka handles\n   512→ * connections very efficiently so this is generally a small cost.\n   513→ * <li><b>CON</b>: Multiple consumers means more requests being sent to the server and slightly less batching of data\n   514→ * which can cause some drop in I/O throughput.\n   515→ * <li><b>CON</b>: The number of total threads across all processes will be limited by the total number of partitions.\n   516→ * </ul>\n   517→ *\n   518→ * <h4>2. Decouple Consumption and Processing</h4>\n   519→ *\n   520→ * Another alternative is to have one or more consumer threads that do all data consumption and hands off\n   521→ * {@link ConsumerRecords} instances to a blocking queue consumed by a pool of processor threads that actually handle\n   522→ * the record processing.\n   523→ *\n   524→ * This option likewise has pros and cons:\n   525→ * <ul>\n   526→ * <li><b>PRO</b>: This option allows independently scaling the number of consumers and processors. This makes it\n   527→ * possible to have a single consumer that feeds many processor threads, avoiding any limitation on partitions.\n   528→ * <li><b>CON</b>: Guaranteeing order across the processors requires particular care as the threads will execute\n   529→ * independently an earlier chunk of data may actually be processed after a later chunk of data just due to the luck of\n   530→ * thread execution timing. One Consumer Per Thread</h4>\n *\n * A simple option is to give each thread its own consumer instance. Here are the pros and cons of this approach:\n * <ul>\n * <li><b>PRO</b>: It is the easiest to implement\n * <li><b>PRO</b>: It is often the fastest as no inter-thread co-ordination is needed\n * <li><b>PRO</b>: It makes in-order processing on a per-partition basis very easy to implement (each thread just\n * processes messages in the order it receives them).\n * <li><b>CON</b>: More consumers means more TCP connections to the cluster (one per thread). In general Kafka handles\n * connections very efficiently so this is generally a small cost.\n * <li><b>CON</b>: Multiple consumers means more requests being sent to the server and slightly less batching of data\n * which can cause some drop in I/O throughput.\n * <li><b>CON</b>: The number of total threads across all processes will be limited by the total number of partitions.\n * </ul>\n *\n * <h4>2. {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_014QvmXATtb39tWwEqBGLcJa","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01HV2ojQJf5fKErfRz1cpYGU","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/documentation.md","content":"# Apache Kafka KafkaConsumer API Reference\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n1. [Overview](#overview)\n2. [Threading Model](#threading-model)\n3. [Core Types](#core-types)\n4. [Consumer Lifecycle](#consumer-lifecycle)\n5. [Subscription and Assignment](#subscription-and-assignment)\n6. [Polling and Data Fetching](#polling-and-data-fetching)\n7. [Offset Management](#offset-management)\n8. [Flow Control and Position Management](#flow-control-and-position-management)\n9. [Rebalancing and Group Coordination](#rebalancing-and-group-coordination)\n10. [Transactional Message Consumption](#transactional-message-consumption)\n11. [Metadata and Monitoring](#metadata-and-monitoring)\n12. [Error Handling](#error-handling)\n13. [Configuration-Driven Behaviors](#configuration-driven-behaviors)\n14. [Common Patterns and Best Practices](#common-patterns-and-best-practices)\n\n---\n\n## Overview\n\n`KafkaConsumer` is a client that consumes records from an Apache Kafka cluster. It transparently handles broker failures, adapts to partition migration, and interacts with brokers to support consumer group-based load balancing.\n\n### Key Characteristics\n\n- **Not Thread-Safe**: The consumer is not thread-safe and access must be synchronized except for `wakeup()`\n- **Single-Threaded Event Loop**: Internally uses an event loop to maintain a single logical consumer thread\n- **Partitioned Topic Support**: Handles both dynamic subscription and manual partition assignment\n- **Group Coordination**: Integrates with the consumer group protocol for distributed load balancing\n- **Flexible Offset Management**: Supports automatic, manual, and external offset storage strategies\n\n### Resource Management\n\nAfter creating a `KafkaConsumer`, you must always call `close()` to avoid resource leaks, as the consumer maintains TCP connections to brokers and background threads for heartbeats and fetch operations.\n\n---\n\n## Threading Model\n\n### Single-Threaded Design\n\nThe Kafka consumer is **not thread-safe**. Only one thread should call consumer methods at a time. Concurrent calls from multiple threads will result in `ConcurrentModificationException`.\n\n**Exception**: The `wakeup()` method is thread-safe and can be called from external threads to interrupt blocking operations.\n\n### Wakeup Mechanism\n\n```java\n// Thread-safe interruption pattern\npublic void wakeup() {\n    // Can be called from any thread\n    // Causes WakeupException in the blocked poll() call\n}\n```\n\n### Thread Interruption\n\nThread interrupts are also supported (will throw `InterruptException`) but are discouraged because they may abort clean consumer shutdown. Use `wakeup()` when possible.\n\n### Multi-Threaded Processing Patterns\n\n#### Pattern 1: One Consumer Per Thread\n- Simplest to implement\n- One consumer instance per thread with dedicated partitions\n- Trade-off: More TCP connections and server requests\n\n#### Pattern 2: Decoupled Consumption and Processing\n- Single consumer thread feeds records to a blocking queue\n- Multiple processor threads consume from the queue\n- Enables independent scaling of consumers and processors\n- Challenge: Ensuring ordering and coordinating commits across threads\n\n---\n\n## Core Types\n\n### KafkaConsumer<K, V>\n\nThe main consumer class for fetching records from Kafka topics.\n\n**Type Parameters:**\n- `K`: Type of the record key\n- `V`: Type of the record value\n\n### ConsumerRecord<K, V>\n\nRepresents a single message fetched from Kafka.\n\n**Key Fields:**\n- `String topic`: Topic from which the record was fetched\n- `int partition`: Partition number within the topic\n- `long offset`: The offset of this record within its partition\n- `long timestamp`: Timestamp of the record (type depends on `timestamp.type` config)\n- `K key`: The record's key (null if no key)\n- `V value`: The record's payload\n- `Headers headers`: Optional headers attached to the record\n- `Optional<Integer> leaderEpoch`: Leader epoch for this record\n\n**Thread Safety Note:** `ConsumerRecord` instances are not thread-safe. Concurrent access by multiple threads may result in undefined behavior. Each individual `Header` instance is read thread-safe.\n\n### ConsumerRecords<K, V>\n\nA collection of consumer records returned by a single `poll()` call.\n\n**Key Methods:**\n- `int count()`: Total number of records\n- `boolean isEmpty()`: Whether collection is empty\n- `Iterable<ConsumerRecord<K, V>> records(TopicPartition partition)`: Records from a specific partition\n- `Set<TopicPartition> partitions()`: All partitions with records\n- `Map<TopicPartition, Long> nextOffsets()`: Next offset to fetch for each partition\n\n### ConsumerRebalanceListener\n\nCallback interface for partition assignment changes.\n\n**Methods:**\n\n```java\npublic interface ConsumerRebalanceListener {\n    /**\n     * Invoked when partitions are revoked during rebalance.\n     * Called before new assignment, allowing cleanup and offset commits.\n     * Under eager rebalancing: called with all assigned partitions\n     * Under cooperative rebalancing: called only with revoked partitions (if non-empty)\n     */\n    void onPartitionsRevoked(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions);\n\n    /**\n     * Invoked after rebalance completes and new partitions are assigned.\n     * Called even if no new partitions were added (to signal rebalance completion).\n     * Use this to initialize positions for newly assigned partitions.\n     */\n    void onPartitionsAssigned(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions);\n\n    /**\n     * Invoked when partitions are lost (not revoked gracefully).\n     * Occurs when session timeout expires or fatal errors occur.\n     * Do not attempt offset commits in this callback.\n     * Default implementation delegates to onPartitionsRevoked().\n     */\n    default void onPartitionsLost(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        onPartitionsRevoked(partitions);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Critical Behavioral Notes:**\n- Callbacks execute in the **user thread** as part of `poll()` calls\n- `onPartitionsRevoked()` always executes before `onPartitionsAssigned()` under normal conditions\n- Exceptions thrown from callbacks propagate to the `poll()` call\n- `WakeupException` and `InterruptException` from nested consumer calls propagate through the callback\n- Rebalances only occur during `poll()` calls, so callbacks only execute during polling\n\n### OffsetAndMetadata\n\nEncapsulates an offset and optional metadata string.\n\n**Constructor:**\n```java\npublic OffsetAndMetadata(long offset)\npublic OffsetAndMetadata(long offset, String metadata)\npublic OffsetAndMetadata(long offset, int leaderEpoch, String metadata)\n```\n\n**Key Concept:** When committing, the offset should be the **next offset to read**, not the last offset processed. If you process offset 4, commit offset 5.\n\n### OffsetCommitCallback\n\nFunctional interface for asynchronous commit completion.\n\n```java\n@FunctionalInterface\npublic interface OffsetCommitCallback {\n    /**\n     * @param offsets Map of offsets that were committed\n     * @param exception null if successful, exception otherwise\n     * @throws CommitFailedException if commit failed and cannot be retried\n     * @throws org.apache.kafka.common.errors.RebalanceInProgressException if rebalance occurred\n     */\n    void onComplete(Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets, Exception exception);\n}\n```\n\n**Execution Context:** Callbacks may execute in any thread calling `poll()`. However, they are guaranteed to execute before any subsequent `commitSync()` call completes.\n\n### OffsetAndTimestamp\n\nResult of timestamp-based offset lookup via `offsetsForTimes()`.\n\n**Fields:**\n- `Long offset`: The offset corresponding to the given timestamp (null if not found)\n- `Long timestamp`: The timestamp of the record at the returned offset\n\n---\n\n## Consumer Lifecycle\n\n### Constructor Variants\n\n#### 1. Configuration Map Constructor\n\n```java\npublic KafkaConsumer(Map<String, Object> configs)\n```\n\n- Takes a map of configuration strings to values\n- Deserializers must be specified in the config map via `key.deserializer` and `value.deserializer` properties\n\n#### 2. Properties Constructor\n\n```java\npublic KafkaConsumer(Properties properties)\n```\n\n- Takes a `Properties` object with configuration\n- Deserializers specified via string-based properties\n\n#### 3. Properties with Explicit Deserializers\n\n```java\npublic KafkaConsumer(Properties properties,\n                     Deserializer<K> keyDeserializer,\n                     Deserializer<V> valueDeserializer)\n```\n\n- Allows passing deserializer instances directly\n- Deserializer `configure()` method will **not** be called when passed directly\n\n#### 4. Config Map with Explicit Deserializers\n\n```java\npublic KafkaConsumer(Map<String, Object> configs,\n                     Deserializer<K> keyDeserializer,\n                     Deserializer<V> valueDeserializer)\n```\n\n**Configuration Note:** Valid configuration strings are documented in `ConsumerConfig` class. Key configs affecting behavior include:\n\n- `bootstrap.servers`: Initial broker list for cluster discovery\n- `group.id`: Consumer group identifier (required for group management)\n- `enable.auto.commit`: Whether to automatically commit offsets (default: true)\n- `auto.commit.interval.ms`: Interval between automatic commits (default: 5000ms)\n- `max.poll.interval.ms`: Maximum time between polls before proactive group exit (default: 300000ms)\n- `session.timeout.ms`: Time before broker considers consumer dead (default: 45000ms)\n- `heartbeat.interval.ms`: Frequency of group coordinator heartbeats (default: 3000ms)\n- `isolation.level`: `read_uncommitted` (default) or `read_committed` for transactional reads\n\n### Close and Cleanup\n\n#### Synchronous Close\n\n```java\npublic void close()\npublic void close(Duration timeout)\n```\n\n- Closes all connections and releases resources\n- Blocks up to the specified timeout (or `default.api.timeout.ms` if not specified)\n- Triggers `onPartitionsRevoked()` callbacks via consumer group protocol\n- Waits for any pending async commits to complete\n- **Must be called** in a finally block or try-with-resources to prevent connection leaks\n\n#### Close with Options\n\n```java\npublic void close(CloseOptions option)\n```\n\n- Supports `leaveGroup()` option for proactive group exit (vs graceful handoff)\n\n**Example:**\n```java\ntry (KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props)) {\n    consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic\"));\n    while (running) {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n        // process records\n    }\n} // close() called automatically\n```\n\n---\n\n## Subscription and Assignment\n\n### Dynamic Subscription (Group Management)\n\n#### Subscribe to Topics with Listener\n\n```java\npublic void subscribe(Collection<String> topics, ConsumerRebalanceListener listener)\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Replaces the previous subscription (not incremental)\n- Enables consumer group coordination and automatic partition assignment\n- Triggers rebalance when:\n  - Partition count for subscribed topics changes\n  - New topic matching subscription is created\n  - Consumer group membership changes\n  - Subscribed topic is deleted\n- Cannot be mixed with manual partition assignment\n\n**Exceptions:**\n- `IllegalArgumentException`: If topics is null, contains nulls, or listener is null\n- `IllegalStateException`: If `subscribe(Pattern)` or `assign()` was previously called without `unsubscribe()`\n\n#### Subscribe to Topics (No Listener)\n\n```java\npublic void subscribe(Collection<String> topics)\n```\n\nEquivalent to `subscribe(topics, ConsumerRebalanceListener.noop())`. No rebalance callbacks are invoked.\n\n#### Subscribe to Topic Pattern\n\n```java\npublic void subscribe(Pattern pattern, ConsumerRebalanceListener listener)\npublic void subscribe(Pattern pattern)\n```\n\nSubscribes to topics matching the regex pattern. New topics matching the pattern are detected through periodic metadata refreshes and trigger rebalances.\n\n**Pattern Validation:** Throws `InvalidRegularExpression` if the pattern is invalid.\n\n#### Subscribe to SubscriptionPattern\n\n```java\npublic void subscribe(SubscriptionPattern pattern, ConsumerRebalanceListener listener)\npublic void subscribe(SubscriptionPattern pattern)\n```\n\nAdvanced pattern type allowing more fine-grained topic matching.\n\n### Manual Assignment (Standalone Mode)\n\n#### Assign Specific Partitions\n\n```java\npublic void assign(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Replaces previous assignment (not incremental)\n- If empty, equivalent to `unsubscribe()`\n- Disables consumer group coordination and rebalancing\n- No rebalance callbacks are triggered\n- Each consumer acts independently\n- Cannot be mixed with dynamic topic subscription\n\n**Offsets:**\n- Initial offsets determined by:\n  1. Last committed offset (if available)\n  2. Offset set via `seek()`\n  3. Reset policy (if no committed offset and no seek)\n\n**Exceptions:**\n- `IllegalArgumentException`: If partitions is null or contains nulls/empty topics\n- `IllegalStateException`: If `subscribe()` was previously called without `unsubscribe()`\n\n### Query Subscription/Assignment\n\n#### Get Current Assignment\n\n```java\npublic Set<TopicPartition> assignment()\n```\n\nReturns partitions currently assigned to this consumer. Empty if using topic subscription and rebalance hasn't completed yet.\n\n#### Get Current Subscription\n\n```java\npublic Set<String> subscription()\n```\n\nReturns topics subscribed to via `subscribe()`. Empty set if using manual assignment or no subscription.\n\n### Unsubscribe\n\n#### Remove All Subscriptions and Assignments\n\n```java\npublic void unsubscribe()\n```\n\n- Clears both topic subscriptions and manual partition assignments\n- Triggers `onPartitionsRevoked()` callback (if using group management)\n- Consumer enters an idle state with no data sources\n\n---\n\n## Polling and Data Fetching\n\n### Poll for Records\n\n#### Main Poll Method\n\n```java\npublic ConsumerRecords<K, V> poll(final Duration timeout)\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n- **Returns immediately** if records are available OR position advances past control records (in `read_committed` mode)\n- **Blocks up to timeout** if no data available, waiting for:\n  - Records to arrive from brokers\n  - Fetch request to complete\n  - Control records or aborted transactions to be skipped\n- **May block longer than timeout** if:\n  - Rebalance callbacks are executing (callbacks don't count toward timeout)\n  - Group coordination is happening\n  - Metadata refresh is in progress\n- Returns empty `ConsumerRecords` if timeout expires with no new data\n\n**Critical Behavioral Note on Rebalancing:**\n- Rebalances only occur during `poll()` calls\n- Callbacks execute as part of `poll()` and may extend total blocking time\n- After `poll()` returns, assignment may have changed\n- The timeout parameter is for network fetches, **not** for callback execution\n\n**Offset Advancement:**\n- `position()` automatically advances as records are fetched\n- If fetching from offset 100-104, position becomes 105 after poll returns\n- Gaps may occur with compacted topics or filtered transactional messages\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `timeout`: Maximum time to wait for data. Must not exceed `Long.MAX_VALUE` milliseconds.\n\n**Return Value:**\n- `ConsumerRecords<K, V>`: Map-like collection of records by partition\n- Empty collection if timeout expires\n- Never null\n\n**Exceptions:**\n- `IllegalStateException`: If no topics/partitions are subscribed/assigned\n- `InvalidOffsetException`: If offset is undefined/out of range and no reset policy configured\n- `WakeupException`: If `wakeup()` was called before/during execution\n- `InterruptException`: If thread was interrupted before/during execution\n- `AuthenticationException`: If authentication fails\n- `AuthorizationException`: If lacking read access to topics or group ID\n- `TimeoutException`: If fetch metadata cannot be retrieved within timeout\n- `InvalidTopicException`: If subscribed topics are invalid\n- `FencedInstanceIdException`: If consumer is fenced by broker (instance ID changed)\n\n**Reset Policy Interaction:**\nThe `auto.offset.reset` configuration controls behavior when offset is invalid:\n- `earliest`: Seek to beginning of partition\n- `latest`: Seek to end of partition\n- `none`: Throw `InvalidOffsetException`\n\n### Poll Semantics Diagram\n\n```\npoll() call\n├─ Check for rebalance needed\n│  └─ Execute ConsumerRebalanceListener callbacks (extends blocking time)\n├─ Fetch data from brokers (up to timeout)\n├─ Skip control records (if read_committed)\n├─ Deserialize records\n└─ Return ConsumerRecords (may be empty)\n\ntime_spent = max(rebalance_callback_time, fetch_time)\n             (NOT timeout + callback_time, callbacks extend the timeout)\n```\n\n### Practical Polling Loop\n\n```java\n// Standard polling loop\nwhile (running) {\n    try {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n        for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n            // Process record\n            processRecord(record);\n        }\n        // Commit after processing\n        consumer.commitAsync();\n    } catch (WakeupException e) {\n        // Expected during shutdown\n        break;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Offset Management\n\n### Core Offset Concepts\n\n#### Position\n- The **offset of the next record to be fetched**\n- Automatically advanced by `poll()` as records are returned\n- Can be manually set via `seek()`\n- Returned by `position(TopicPartition)`\n\n**Key Relationship:** If `position()` is N, the next `poll()` will fetch starting from offset N.\n\n#### Committed Offset\n- The **offset of the next record to read** after restart\n- Stored durably by Kafka broker\n- Retrieved by `committed(Set<TopicPartition>)`\n- Updated via `commitSync()`, `commitAsync()`, or automatic commits\n\n**Commitment Rule:** When committing, the offset should be the **next offset to read**, not the last offset processed.\n\n```java\n// Correct: commit the offset of the next message to read\nconsumer.commitSync(Collections.singletonMap(\n    partition,\n    new OffsetAndMetadata(lastProcessedRecord.offset() + 1)\n));\n\n// Or use ConsumerRecords.nextOffsets()\nconsumer.commitSync(records.nextOffsets());\n```\n\n#### Beginning and End Offsets\n- Beginning offset: The earliest offset available in a partition\n- End offset: The offset **after** the last message\n- For `read_committed`: End offset is the LSO (Last Stable Offset)\n\n### Automatic Offset Commits\n\n#### Configuration\n\n- `enable.auto.commit`: Set to `true` to enable (default)\n- `auto.commit.interval.ms`: Time between commits (default: 5000ms)\n\n#### Behavior\n\n- Commits the current `position()` automatically at interval\n- Commits happen asynchronously (not during `poll()` calls)\n- If consumer crashes between commits, messages between last commit and crash may be reprocessed\n- Safe for \"at-least-once\" delivery semantics\n- All records from `poll()` must be processed before next `poll()` call to avoid committed offset advancing ahead of processed records\n\n#### Rebalance Behavior\n\n- Auto-commits are triggered before rebalance starts\n- A final commit happens during `close()`\n\n### Manual Synchronous Commits\n\n#### Commit All Consumed Offsets\n\n```java\npublic void commitSync()\npublic void commitSync(Duration timeout)\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Blocks until commit succeeds or error occurs\n- Commits the current `position()` for all assigned partitions\n- Uses `default.api.timeout.ms` if no timeout specified\n- Retries on transient errors until timeout\n\n**Return:** No return value (void)\n\n#### Commit Specific Offsets\n\n```java\npublic void commitSync(Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets)\npublic void commitSync(Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets, Duration timeout)\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Commits explicitly specified offsets per partition\n- Allows fine-grained control over which offsets are committed\n- Offsets must be for currently assigned partitions (if using group management)\n- Map is copied internally; safe to mutate after returning\n\n**Use Case:** Commit after processing each partition's records separately\n```java\nConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\nfor (TopicPartition partition : records.partitions()) {\n    List<ConsumerRecord<String, String>> partitionRecords = records.records(partition);\n    for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : partitionRecords) {\n        processRecord(record);\n    }\n    // Commit after this partition is fully processed\n    long nextOffset = records.nextOffsets().get(partition).offset();\n    consumer.commitSync(Collections.singletonMap(\n        partition,\n        new OffsetAndMetadata(nextOffset)\n    ));\n}\n```\n\n**Exceptions:**\n- `CommitFailedException`: Commit failed and cannot be retried (fatal in group management)\n- `RebalanceInProgressException`: Consumer in middle of rebalance\n- `WakeupException`: `wakeup()` called\n- `InterruptException`: Thread interrupted\n- `TimeoutException`: Timeout expired before commit\n\n### Manual Asynchronous Commits\n\n#### Commit All Consumed Offsets (Async)\n\n```java\npublic void commitAsync()\npublic void commitAsync(OffsetCommitCallback callback)\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Returns immediately without blocking\n- Commits the current `position()` for all assigned partitions\n- Callback invoked when commit completes (or immediately if null)\n- Multiple async commits are ordered; callbacks invoked in order\n- Async commits complete before subsequent `commitSync()` calls return\n\n#### Commit Specific Offsets (Async)\n\n```java\npublic void commitAsync(Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets,\n                        OffsetCommitCallback callback)\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Commits explicitly specified offsets asynchronously\n- Callback receives the committed offsets and any exception\n\n**Callback Example:**\n```java\nconsumer.commitAsync(new OffsetCommitCallback() {\n    public void onComplete(Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets, Exception exception) {\n        if (exception != null) {\n            log.error(\"Commit failed for offsets: \" + offsets, exception);\n        } else {\n            log.info(\"Commit succeeded for offsets: \" + offsets);\n        }\n    }\n});\n```\n\n**Callback Exceptions:**\n- `CommitFailedException`: Cannot be retried\n- `RebalanceInProgressException`: Can retry after rebalance\n- `WakeupException`: Can rethrow or ignore\n- `InterruptException`: Can rethrow or ignore\n\n### Offset Reset Policies\n\n#### Configuration\n\n- `auto.offset.reset`: How to initialize offset if not found\n\n#### Behavior\n\nApplied when:\n- No committed offset exists for partition\n- Offset is out of range (log deleted, partition recreated)\n- Explicit offset not set via `seek()`\n\n#### Options\n\n- `earliest`: Start from beginning offset (offset 0 or first available)\n- `latest`: Start from end offset (next offset after last message)\n- `none`: Throw `InvalidOffsetException` (fail fast, explicit offset required)\n\n### Query Committed Offsets\n\n#### Get Committed Offsets\n\n```java\npublic Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> committed(Set<TopicPartition> partitions)\npublic Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> committed(Set<TopicPartition> partitions,\n                                                        Duration timeout)\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Returns committed offsets for specified partitions\n- Makes remote call to broker to fetch latest committed values\n- Returns null for partitions with no committed offset\n- Map key is `TopicPartition`, value is `OffsetAndMetadata` or null\n- Blocks until commit status retrieved or timeout expires\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `partitions`: Which partitions to query\n- `timeout`: Maximum wait time (uses `default.api.timeout.ms` if not specified)\n\n**Return:** Map with entries only for partitions with committed offsets\n\n---\n\n## Flow Control and Position Management\n\n### Pause and Resume\n\n#### Pause Consuming from Partitions\n\n```java\npublic void pause(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Pauses fetching from specified partitions\n- Records already fetched remain available via `poll()`\n- `poll()` will not fetch new records from paused partitions\n- Already-fetched records must be consumed before resuming\n\n**Use Cases:**\n- Back-pressure handling: Pause faster partitions while slower ones catch up\n- Stream processing: Pause input while processing previous batch\n- Rebalancing: Pause to prevent new data during critical sections\n\n#### Resume Consuming from Partitions\n\n```java\npublic void resume(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Resumes fetching from previously paused partitions\n- No-op if partition was not paused\n- Next `poll()` will fetch new records from resumed partitions\n\n#### Query Paused Partitions\n\n```java\npublic Set<TopicPartition> paused()\n```\n\n**Return:** Set of currently paused partitions\n\n### Position Control\n\n#### Seek to Specific Offset\n\n```java\npublic void seek(TopicPartition partition, long offset)\npublic void seek(TopicPartition partition, OffsetAndMetadata offsetAndMetadata)\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Sets the `position()` to the specified offset\n- Effective on next `poll()` call\n- Multiple seeks for same partition replace previous seeks\n- Only affects fetching, not committed offset\n\n**Variant with Metadata:**\n- Second form includes leader epoch information\n- Preserves epoch across consumer restarts for data consistency\n- Epoch obtained from `ConsumerRecord#leaderEpoch()` or `ConsumerRecords#nextOffsets()`\n\n**Exceptions:**\n- `IllegalArgumentException`: If offset is negative\n- `IllegalStateException`: If partition not assigned\n\n**Use Case:** Restart from custom offset store\n```java\nconsumer.assign(Arrays.asList(new TopicPartition(\"topic\", 0)));\nlong savedOffset = externalOffsetStore.getOffset(\"topic\", 0);\nconsumer.seek(new TopicPartition(\"topic\", 0), savedOffset);\n```\n\n#### Seek to Beginning\n\n```java\npublic void seekToBeginning(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Sets position to the earliest offset in each partition\n- Lazy evaluation: actual seek happens during `poll()` or `position()` call\n- Empty partition list seeks all assigned partitions\n- Allows re-consuming all available data\n\n#### Seek to End\n\n```java\npublic void seekToEnd(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Sets position to the end offset (first offset after last message)\n- Lazy evaluation: actual seek happens during `poll()` or `position()` call\n- Empty partition list seeks all assigned partitions\n- Useful for skipping backlog and consuming only new data\n\n**Transactional Behavior:**\n- With `isolation.level=read_committed`: Seeks to LSO (Last Stable Offset), not absolute end\n- LSO is the offset of the first message in an open transaction\n- Allows reading only committed transactional messages\n\n#### Get Current Position\n\n```java\npublic long position(TopicPartition partition)\npublic long position(TopicPartition partition, final Duration timeout)\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Returns the offset of the next record that will be fetched\n- May issue remote call if position not yet determined\n- Blocks until position determined or timeout expires\n- Triggers lazy seeks set via `seekToBeginning()` or `seekToEnd()`\n\n**Return:** The current position (next offset to fetch)\n\n**Exceptions:**\n- `IllegalStateException`: If partition not assigned\n- `InvalidOffsetException`: If position undefined (no committed offset, no seek, out of range)\n- `TimeoutException`: If position cannot be determined before timeout\n\n### Timestamp-Based Offset Lookup\n\n#### Search for Offsets by Timestamp\n\n```java\npublic Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndTimestamp> offsetsForTimes(Map<TopicPartition, Long> timestampsToSearch)\npublic Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndTimestamp> offsetsForTimes(Map<TopicPartition, Long> timestampsToSearch,\n                                                               Duration timeout)\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Finds the offset for each partition's first message with timestamp >= given timestamp\n- Makes remote call to brokers\n- Returns null if timestamp not found (no message with that timestamp exists)\n- Blocks until offsets retrieved or timeout expires\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `timestampsToSearch`: Map of partition to timestamp (milliseconds since epoch)\n- `timeout`: Maximum wait time\n\n**Return:** Map of partition to `OffsetAndTimestamp` (null if not found)\n\n**Use Case:** Seek to messages from specific time\n```java\nMap<TopicPartition, Long> timestampsToSearch = new HashMap<>();\ntimestampsToSearch.put(partition, System.currentTimeMillis() - 3600000); // 1 hour ago\n\nMap<TopicPartition, OffsetAndTimestamp> offsets = consumer.offsetsForTimes(timestampsToSearch);\nfor (Map.Entry<TopicPartition, OffsetAndTimestamp> entry : offsets.entrySet()) {\n    if (entry.getValue() != null) {\n        consumer.seek(entry.getKey(), entry.getValue().offset());\n    }\n}\n```\n\n#### Get Beginning Offsets\n\n```java\npublic Map<TopicPartition, Long> beginningOffsets(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)\npublic Map<TopicPartition, Long> beginningOffsets(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions,\n                                                  Duration timeout)\n```\n\n**Return:** Map of partition to earliest available offset\n\n**Note:** Does not seek; only returns the offset value.\n\n#### Get End Offsets\n\n```java\npublic Map<TopicPartition, Long> endOffsets(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)\npublic Map<TopicPartition, Long> endOffsets(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions,\n                                           Duration timeout)\n```\n\n**Return:** Map of partition to end offset (first offset after last message)\n\n**Transactional Note:** With `isolation.level=read_committed`, returns LSO instead of absolute end.\n\n---\n\n## Rebalancing and Group Coordination\n\n### Consumer Groups Overview\n\nA consumer group is a set of consumer instances sharing the same `group.id` that collectively consume a topic's partitions. Kafka automatically assigns partitions to group members.\n\n**Key Properties:**\n- Only one consumer group member receives each partition\n- Partitions distribute across group members\n- Instances can dynamically join/leave\n- Broker manages group coordination and partition rebalancing\n\n### Group Membership and Lifecycle\n\n#### Initial Join\n\n- Consumer joins group on first `poll()` call after `subscribe()`\n- Triggers a rebalance to redistribute partitions\n- Assignment delayed until rebalance completes\n\n#### Session Management\n\n**session.timeout.ms:** Time before broker considers consumer dead (default: 45000ms)\n- If no heartbeat received for this duration, consumer removed from group\n- Triggers rebalance with other members\n\n**heartbeat.interval.ms:** Frequency of group heartbeats (default: 3000ms)\n- Recommended: `session.timeout.ms / 3`\n- Sent periodically; failure to send triggers timeout\n\n**max.poll.interval.ms:** Maximum time between polls (default: 300000ms)\n- If consumer doesn't call `poll()` within this interval, proactively exits group\n- Prevents \"livelock\" where consumer sends heartbeats but makes no progress\n- Exceeding this causes `CommitFailedException` on commit attempts\n\n#### Proactive Group Exit\n\nWhen consumer exceeds `max.poll.interval.ms`:\n1. Consumer proactively leaves the group\n2. `onPartitionsRevoked()` triggered on next `poll()` call\n3. Partitions reassigned to other group members\n4. Subsequent commits fail with `CommitFailedException`\n\nThis is a **safety mechanism** ensuring only active members commit offsets.\n\n### Rebalance Triggering Events\n\nRebalances occur when:\n- New consumer joins group (detected during heartbeat)\n- Consumer leaves group (gracefully or timeout)\n- Partition count changes for subscribed topics\n- Subscribed topic created/deleted\n- New topic matching subscribed pattern created\n- Consumer fails to send heartbeat\n- `enforceRebalance()` called\n\n### Rebalance Protocols\n\n#### Classic (Eager) Protocol\n- **Name:** `GroupProtocol.CLASSIC`\n- `onPartitionsRevoked()` called with **full assignment** (all partitions revoked)\n- All members must participate before assignment completes\n- More disruptive, all members must rebalance simultaneously\n\n#### Cooperative (Incremental) Protocol\n- **Name:** `GroupProtocol.CONSUMER` or cooperative assignments\n- `onPartitionsRevoked()` called only with **revoked partitions** (if non-empty)\n- Members can continue consuming stable partitions during rebalance\n- Less disruptive, only revoked partitions stop temporarily\n\n**Configuration:** `group.protocol` (legacy: `partition.assignment.strategy`)\n\n### Rebalance Listener Callbacks\n\n#### Callback Execution Order\n\nUnder normal conditions:\n1. **onPartitionsRevoked()** - Revoked partitions leaving this consumer\n2. *Rebalance at broker*\n3. **onPartitionsAssigned()** - New partitions assigned to this consumer\n\n#### onPartitionsRevoked Semantics\n\n```java\npublic void onPartitionsRevoked(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n    // Save offsets, flush caches, release resources\n    // Called with full assignment under eager rebalance\n    // Called with subset under cooperative rebalance\n}\n```\n\n**Recommended Actions:**\n- Commit offsets to Kafka or external store\n- Flush any accumulated state\n- Close external connections tied to partitions\n- Clear partition-specific caches\n\n#### onPartitionsAssigned Semantics\n\n```java\npublic void onPartitionsAssigned(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n    // Initialize positions, load external state, warm caches\n    // Called even if partitions is empty (signals rebalance completion)\n}\n```\n\n**Recommended Actions:**\n- Initialize position for new partitions\n- Load state from external offset store\n- Warm up partition-specific caches\n- Do NOT start consuming yet (happens automatically after callback returns)\n\n**Guaranteed:** All revocations complete before any member's `onPartitionsAssigned()` executes.\n\n#### onPartitionsLost Semantics\n\n```java\npublic void onPartitionsLost(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n    // Handle unexpected loss, don't commit offsets\n    // Partitions may already belong to other members\n}\n```\n\n**When Invoked:**\n- Session timeout occurred\n- Fatal error received from broker\n- Not a graceful revocation\n\n**Action:** Do not attempt to commit offsets; partitions may already belong to others.\n\n### Enforce Rebalance\n\n#### Trigger Rebalance Manually\n\n```java\npublic void enforceRebalance()\npublic void enforceRebalance(final String reason)\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Signals coordinator that rebalance should occur\n- Rebalance happens on next `poll()` call\n- Useful for updating group composition without timeout\n\n**Use Case:** Remove consumer from group on-demand without waiting for timeout\n```java\nconsumer.enforceRebalance();\ntry {\n    consumer.poll(Duration.ofSeconds(1)); // Wait for rebalance\n} catch (InterruptException e) {\n    // May be interrupted during rebalance\n}\n```\n\n### Group Metadata\n\n#### Get Group Information\n\n```java\npublic ConsumerGroupMetadata groupMetadata()\n```\n\n**Return:** Metadata about current group membership including:\n- Group ID\n- Generation ID\n- Member ID\n- Partition assignment strategy\n\n**Use Case:** Pass to transactional producers for exactly-once semantics\n```java\nConsumerGroupMetadata metadata = consumer.groupMetadata();\n// Use in producer transactions to coordinate exactly-once processing\n```\n\n---\n\n## Transactional Message Consumption\n\n### Isolation Levels\n\nThe `isolation.level` configuration controls how transactional messages are read.\n\n#### read_uncommitted (Default)\n\n- Reads all messages including uncommitted transactional messages\n- No client-side buffering\n- Most throughput\n- Messages may roll back if transaction aborts\n\n#### read_committed\n\n- Reads only committed transactional messages\n- Skips aborted transaction messages\n- LSO (Last Stable Offset) boundaries\n- Better consistency guarantees\n\n### Reading in read_committed Mode\n\n#### Message Filtering\n\n- Consumer automatically filters out aborted transaction markers\n- Transaction commit/abort markers not returned to application (but consume offsets)\n- Gap in offsets indicates filtered messages\n\n**Example:**\n```\nOffsets: 1, 2, 3, [4-6 aborted and filtered], 7, 8, 9\nReturned: 1, 2, 3, 7, 8, 9\n```\n\n#### Last Stable Offset (LSO)\n\nThe LSO is the offset of the first message in an open transaction. Consumer blocks at LSO until:\n- Transaction commits (LSO advances)\n- Transaction aborts (transaction filtered, LSO advances)\n- Timeout occurs\n\n**Effect on Offset Queries:**\n- `position()` does not advance past LSO\n- `seekToEnd()` seeks to LSO, not absolute end\n- `endOffsets()` returns LSO, not absolute end\n\n#### No Client-Side Buffering\n\nUnlike `read_uncommitted`:\n- Messages are not buffered waiting for transaction commit\n- Consumer simply stops at LSO if transaction still open\n- Next `poll()` returns empty until LSO advances\n\n### Consuming Exactly-Once with Transactions\n\n```java\n// Consumer only reads committed messages\nProperties props = new Properties();\nprops.setProperty(\"isolation.level\", \"read_committed\");\n\n// Producer writes transactions\n// Consumer reads committed messages atomically\n// Coordinate via ConsumerGroupMetadata for exactly-once processing\n```\n\n---\n\n## Metadata and Monitoring\n\n### Partition Information\n\n#### Get Partition Metadata\n\n```java\npublic List<PartitionInfo> partitionsFor(String topic)\npublic List<PartitionInfo> partitionsFor(String topic, Duration timeout)\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Returns metadata about all partitions for a topic\n- Makes remote call if metadata not cached\n- Returns empty list if topic doesn't exist\n\n**Return Value:** List of `PartitionInfo` objects containing:\n- Partition ID\n- Leader broker ID\n- Replica broker IDs\n- In-sync replica (ISR) broker IDs\n\n#### List All Topics\n\n```java\npublic Map<String, List<PartitionInfo>> listTopics()\npublic Map<String, List<PartitionInfo>> listTopics(Duration timeout)\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Returns metadata for all topics in cluster\n- May issue remote call\n- Blocks until metadata retrieved or timeout expires\n\n**Return:** Map from topic name to partition list\n\n### Metrics\n\n#### Get Consumer Metrics\n\n```java\npublic Map<MetricName, ? extends Metric> metrics()\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Returns all metrics tracked by consumer\n- Includes:\n  - Fetch rates and latencies\n  - Commit success/failure rates\n  - Consumer lag per partition\n  - Rebalance metrics\n  - Network metrics\n\n**Use Case:** Custom monitoring and alerting\n```java\nMap<MetricName, ? extends Metric> metrics = consumer.metrics();\nfor (Map.Entry<MetricName, ? extends Metric> entry : metrics.entrySet()) {\n    MetricName name = entry.getKey();\n    double value = entry.getValue().value();\n    // Report metric\n}\n```\n\n### Consumer Lag\n\n#### Get Current Lag\n\n```java\npublic OptionalLong currentLag(TopicPartition topicPartition)\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Returns the difference between end offset and current position\n- `OptionalLong.empty()` if lag cannot be determined\n- Non-blocking call\n\n**Semantics:**\n```\nlag = endOffset - position()\n\n// If consumer at position 100, end offset 150:\n// lag = 150 - 100 = 50 messages behind\n```\n\n**Use Case:** Detect slow consumers\n```java\nOptionalLong lag = consumer.currentLag(partition);\nif (lag.isPresent() && lag.getAsLong() > 10000) {\n    log.warn(\"Consumer lagging by \" + lag.getAsLong() + \" messages\");\n}\n```\n\n### Client Telemetry\n\n#### Get Client Instance ID\n\n```java\npublic Uuid clientInstanceId(Duration timeout)\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Returns unique ID for this consumer instance\n- Used for correlating telemetry\n- Requires telemetry enabled: `enable.metrics.push=true`\n- First call generates ID via remote request\n- Blocks until ID obtained or timeout expires\n\n**Exception:**\n- `IllegalStateException`: If telemetry not enabled\n\n---\n\n## Error Handling\n\n### Exception Hierarchy\n\nAll Kafka exceptions extend `KafkaException`. Consumer-specific exceptions include:\n\n### Recoverable Errors (May Retry)\n\n#### RebalanceInProgressException\n\n**When:** Rebalance is in progress when commit attempted\n\n**Handling:**\n```java\ntry {\n    consumer.commitSync();\n} catch (RebalanceInProgressException e) {\n    // Wait for rebalance to complete via poll()\n    consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n    // Retry commit after rebalance\n    consumer.commitSync();\n}\n```\n\n#### TimeoutException\n\n**When:** Operation doesn't complete within timeout\n\n**Handling:**\n- Network temporarily unavailable\n- Broker slow to respond\n- Usually transient; retry with longer timeout\n\n### Fatal Errors (Cannot Retry)\n\n#### CommitFailedException\n\n**When:** Commit attempted on partitions no longer assigned\n\n**Triggers:**\n- Consumer exceeds `max.poll.interval.ms` (proactive group exit)\n- Rebalance occurred, partitions reassigned\n- Consumer fenced by broker\n- Using group management, partition lost\n\n**Handling:**\n```java\ntry {\n    consumer.commitSync();\n} catch (CommitFailedException e) {\n    log.error(\"Commit failed - consumer likely fenced or partitions reassigned\");\n    // May attempt to recover:\n    // 1. Wait for rebalance via poll()\n    // 2. Check if partitions still assigned\n    // 3. Verify max.poll.interval.ms not exceeded\n}\n```\n\n**Prevention:**\n- Call `poll()` at least every `max.poll.interval.ms`\n- Process records quickly\n- Move expensive processing to separate thread pool with pause/resume\n\n#### InvalidOffsetException\n\n**When:** Offset is invalid (out of range, deleted)\n\n**Triggers:**\n- Committed offset before partition start (log deleted)\n- Committed offset after partition end\n- No offset committed and `auto.offset.reset=none`\n\n**Handling:**\n```java\ntry {\n    consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n} catch (InvalidOffsetException e) {\n    // Recover by seeking to valid offset\n    TopicPartition partition = e.topicPartition(); // if available\n    consumer.seek(partition, consumer.beginningOffsets(\n        Collections.singleton(partition)).get(partition));\n}\n```\n\n### Interruption and Wakeup\n\n#### WakeupException\n\n**When:** `wakeup()` called before/during blocking operation\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Causes immediate return from blocking operations\n- `WakeupException` thrown to caller\n- Safe to call from any thread\n\n**Handling:**\n```java\ntry {\n    ConsumerRecords<K, V> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofSeconds(1));\n} catch (WakeupException e) {\n    if (shutdownRequested) {\n        break; // Expected, proceed with shutdown\n    } else {\n        throw e; // Unexpected, propagate\n    }\n}\n```\n\n#### InterruptException\n\n**When:** Thread interrupted before/during blocking operation\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Thread's interrupt flag is checked\n- `InterruptException` thrown\n- Discouraged; use `wakeup()` instead\n\n**Handling:** Same as `WakeupException`\n\n### Authentication and Authorization\n\n#### AuthenticationException\n\n**When:** Credentials invalid or missing\n\n**Triggers:**\n- Wrong credentials\n- Credentials expired\n- SASL mechanism error\n\n**Handling:** Verify credentials and configuration\n\n#### AuthorizationException\n\n**When:** User lacks permission to access resource\n\n**Triggers:**\n- No read permission for topic\n- No read permission for group ID\n- ACL denies operation\n\n**Handling:** Verify user ACLs\n\n### Instance Fencing\n\n#### FencedInstanceIdException\n\n**When:** Another consumer instance with same instance ID joined group\n\n**Causes:**\n- Duplicate instance IDs (instance.id configuration)\n- Consumer restarted with same ID while previous instance still active\n- Broker replaced older instance with new one\n\n**Handling:**\n```java\ntry {\n    consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n} catch (FencedInstanceIdException e) {\n    log.error(\"Consumer instance fenced by broker\");\n    consumer.close();\n    System.exit(1); // Force restart with fresh instance\n}\n```\n\n### Deserialization Errors\n\n**When:** Deserializer fails for key/value\n\n**Exception:** Wrapped in `SerializationException` (extends `KafkaException`)\n\n**Handling:**\n- Catch and log\n- Skip message or fail fast depending on requirements\n- Consider dead-letter queues\n\n---\n\n## Configuration-Driven Behaviors\n\n### Key Configuration Parameters\n\n#### bootstrap.servers (Required)\n\n- Initial broker list: `host1:port1,host2:port2`\n- Used only for cluster discovery\n- All brokers discovered via metadata\n\n#### group.id (Required for Group Management)\n\n- Consumer group identifier\n- Empty string = standalone mode (no group coordination)\n- All consumers with same group.id form a group\n\n#### enable.auto.commit (Default: true)\n\n- `true`: Automatic offset commits at interval\n- `false`: Manual commit required\n- Commits position() automatically\n\n#### auto.commit.interval.ms (Default: 5000)\n\n- Interval between automatic commits\n- Only used if `enable.auto.commit=true`\n\n#### max.poll.interval.ms (Default: 300000)\n\n- Maximum milliseconds between poll() calls\n- Consumer proactively exits group if exceeded\n- Prevents livelock detection\n\n#### session.timeout.ms (Default: 45000)\n\n- Maximum milliseconds without heartbeat before removal\n- Should be >= 1.5 * heartbeat.interval.ms\n\n#### heartbeat.interval.ms (Default: 3000)\n\n- Milliseconds between group heartbeats\n- Should be <= session.timeout.ms / 3\n\n#### isolation.level\n\n- `read_uncommitted` (default): Read all messages\n- `read_committed`: Read only committed transactional messages\n\n#### auto.offset.reset\n\n- `earliest`: Start from beginning\n- `latest`: Start from end\n- `none`: Throw exception if no committed offset\n\n#### fetch.min.bytes (Default: 1)\n\n- Minimum bytes broker accumulates before returning\n- Trade-off between latency and throughput\n\n#### fetch.max.wait.ms (Default: 500)\n\n- Maximum milliseconds broker waits for fetch.min.bytes\n- Returned early if data available\n\n#### max.poll.records (Default: 500)\n\n- Maximum records returned per poll()\n- Helps bound processing time per iteration\n\n---\n\n## Common Patterns and Best Practices\n\n### Pattern 1: Basic Subscription with Auto-Commit\n\nSimplest pattern suitable for non-critical applications.\n\n```java\nProperties props = new Properties();\nprops.setProperty(\"bootstrap.servers\", \"localhost:9092\");\nprops.setProperty(\"group.id\", \"my-group\");\nprops.setProperty(\"enable.auto.commit\", \"true\");\nprops.setProperty(\"auto.commit.interval.ms\", \"1000\");\nprops.setProperty(\"key.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\nprops.setProperty(\"value.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\n\ntry (KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props)) {\n    consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic1\", \"topic2\"));\n\n    while (true) {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n        for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n            System.out.printf(\"topic=%s partition=%d offset=%d key=%s value=%s%n\",\n                record.topic(), record.partition(), record.offset(),\n                record.key(), record.value());\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**When to Use:**\n- Non-critical data where message loss acceptable\n- Consistent low latency important\n- At-least-once semantics sufficient\n\n### Pattern 2: Manual Synchronous Commits\n\nEnsures all records processed before offset committed.\n\n```java\nProperties props = new Properties();\nprops.setProperty(\"bootstrap.servers\", \"localhost:9092\");\nprops.setProperty(\"group.id\", \"my-group\");\nprops.setProperty(\"enable.auto.commit\", \"false\");\nprops.setProperty(\"key.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\nprops.setProperty(\"value.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\n\ntry (KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props)) {\n    consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic1\"));\n\n    while (true) {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n        for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n            processRecord(record); // Process before commit\n        }\n        try {\n            consumer.commitSync(); // Commit after all processed\n        } catch (CommitFailedException e) {\n            log.error(\"Commit failed\", e);\n            // Handle: may need to restart\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Semantics:** Guarantees at-least-once delivery\n\n**When to Use:**\n- Data integrity important\n- Can tolerate occasional reprocessing\n- Batch processing workflows\n\n### Pattern 3: Manual Offset Commits with Rebalance Listener\n\nHandles offset persistence during rebalancing.\n\n```java\nclass OffsetTracker implements ConsumerRebalanceListener {\n    private final KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer;\n    private final Map<TopicPartition, Long> offsets = new HashMap<>();\n\n    @Override\n    public void onPartitionsRevoked(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        // Save offsets before losing ownership\n        for (TopicPartition partition : partitions) {\n            long offset = consumer.position(partition);\n            externalStore.saveOffset(partition, offset);\n            log.info(\"Saved offset for \" + partition + \": \" + offset);\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void onPartitionsAssigned(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        // Restore offsets after gaining ownership\n        for (TopicPartition partition : partitions) {\n            long offset = externalStore.getOffset(partition);\n            if (offset >= 0) {\n                consumer.seek(partition, offset);\n                log.info(\"Restored offset for \" + partition + \": \" + offset);\n            } else {\n                consumer.seekToBeginning(Collections.singleton(partition));\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nProperties props = new Properties();\nprops.setProperty(\"bootstrap.servers\", \"localhost:9092\");\nprops.setProperty(\"group.id\", \"my-group\");\nprops.setProperty(\"enable.auto.commit\", \"false\");\n// ... deserializers ...\n\ntry (KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props)) {\n    consumer.subscribe(\n        Arrays.asList(\"topic1\"),\n        new OffsetTracker(consumer)\n    );\n\n    while (true) {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n        for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n            processRecord(record);\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Benefits:**\n- Offsets can be stored in database alongside processing results\n- Exactly-once semantics if external store is transactional\n- Decoupled from Kafka offset storage\n\n### Pattern 4: Decoupled Consumption and Processing\n\nSeparates consumption from processing for better resource utilization.\n\n```java\nBlockingQueue<ConsumerRecord<String, String>> recordQueue =\n    new LinkedBlockingQueue<>(10000);\n\n// Consumer thread\nThread consumerThread = new Thread(() -> {\n    Properties props = new Properties();\n    props.setProperty(\"bootstrap.servers\", \"localhost:9092\");\n    props.setProperty(\"group.id\", \"my-group\");\n    props.setProperty(\"enable.auto.commit\", \"false\");\n    // ... deserializers ...\n\n    try (KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props)) {\n        consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic1\"));\n        Set<TopicPartition> assigned = new HashSet<>();\n\n        while (!Thread.interrupted()) {\n            ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n\n            // Track assignment\n            assigned.addAll(records.partitions());\n\n            for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n                recordQueue.offer(record);\n            }\n\n            // Commit only processed records\n            try {\n                consumer.commitSync();\n            } catch (CommitFailedException e) {\n                log.warn(\"Commit failed, may reprocess\", e);\n            }\n        }\n    } catch (WakeupException e) {\n        // Expected on shutdown\n    }\n});\n\n// Worker threads\nfor (int i = 0; i < 4; i++) {\n    new Thread(() -> {\n        while (true) {\n            try {\n                ConsumerRecord<String, String> record = recordQueue.poll(1, TimeUnit.SECONDS);\n                if (record != null) {\n                    processRecord(record); // Expensive processing\n                }\n            } catch (InterruptedException e) {\n                break;\n            }\n        }\n    }).start();\n}\n\n// Shutdown\nconsumerThread.start();\n// Later...\nconsumerThread.interrupt();\nconsumer.wakeup();\n```\n\n**Benefits:**\n- Processing doesn't block consumption\n- Scales independently\n- Can recover from transient processing failures\n\n**Challenges:**\n- Harder to guarantee message ordering\n- Complex offset management across threads\n- Risk of processing timeout during max.poll.interval.ms\n\n### Pattern 5: Manual Partition Assignment (Standalone Mode)\n\nDirect control over partitions without group coordination.\n\n```java\nProperties props = new Properties();\nprops.setProperty(\"bootstrap.servers\", \"localhost:9092\");\nprops.setProperty(\"key.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\nprops.setProperty(\"value.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\n// No group.id required for standalone mode\n\ntry (KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props)) {\n    // Manually assign specific partitions\n    consumer.assign(Arrays.asList(\n        new TopicPartition(\"topic1\", 0),\n        new TopicPartition(\"topic1\", 1)\n    ));\n\n    // Seek to specific offset\n    consumer.seek(new TopicPartition(\"topic1\", 0), 1000);\n\n    while (true) {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n        for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n            processRecord(record);\n        }\n        consumer.commitAsync();\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**When to Use:**\n- Precise partition control needed\n- External partition assignment\n- Testing and debugging\n- Standalone tool (not part of consumer group)\n\n### Pattern 6: Seeking and Time-Based Consumption\n\nConsume from specific points in partition history.\n\n```java\ntry (KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props)) {\n    consumer.assign(Arrays.asList(new TopicPartition(\"topic1\", 0)));\n\n    // Seek to beginning\n    consumer.seekToBeginning(consumer.assignment());\n\n    // Seek to specific timestamp (1 hour ago)\n    Map<TopicPartition, Long> timestampsToSearch = new HashMap<>();\n    timestampsToSearch.put(new TopicPartition(\"topic1\", 0),\n                          System.currentTimeMillis() - 3600000);\n\n    Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndTimestamp> offsets = consumer.offsetsForTimes(timestampsToSearch);\n    for (TopicPartition partition : consumer.assignment()) {\n        OffsetAndTimestamp offset = offsets.get(partition);\n        if (offset != null) {\n            consumer.seek(partition, offset.offset());\n        }\n    }\n\n    while (true) {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n        // Process records from desired starting point\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Use Cases:**\n- Replay historical data\n- Skip corrupted segments\n- Test impact of recent changes\n- Disaster recovery\n\n### Pattern 7: Exactly-Once Processing with External State\n\nCoordinate offset commits with processing results.\n\n```java\nProperties props = new Properties();\nprops.setProperty(\"isolation.level\", \"read_committed\");\nprops.setProperty(\"enable.auto.commit\", \"false\");\n// ... other config ...\n\ntry (KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props)) {\n    consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"transactions\"));\n\n    while (true) {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n\n        // Process in partition batches for ordering\n        for (TopicPartition partition : records.partitions()) {\n            List<ConsumerRecord<String, String>> partitionRecords =\n                records.records(partition);\n\n            // Start transaction\n            database.beginTransaction();\n            try {\n                for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : partitionRecords) {\n                    // Process and store results\n                    processAndStore(record);\n                }\n\n                // Atomically commit result and offset\n                long nextOffset = records.nextOffsets().get(partition).offset();\n                database.saveOffset(partition, nextOffset);\n                database.commit();\n\n                // Now safe to commit to Kafka\n                consumer.commitSync(Collections.singletonMap(\n                    partition,\n                    new OffsetAndMetadata(nextOffset)\n                ));\n            } catch (Exception e) {\n                database.rollback();\n                log.error(\"Processing failed\", e);\n                // Will retry on next poll\n                throw new RuntimeException(e);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Guarantees:** Exactly-once message processing (if external store is transactional)\n\n### Pattern 8: Pause/Resume for Back-Pressure\n\nManage consumption rate with pausing.\n\n```java\ntry (KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props)) {\n    consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic1\"));\n\n    BlockingQueue<ConsumerRecord<String, String>> queue =\n        new LinkedBlockingQueue<>(1000);\n\n    while (true) {\n        // Check queue fullness\n        if (queue.size() > 900) {\n            // Pause to prevent buffer overflow\n            consumer.pause(consumer.assignment());\n            log.info(\"Paused consumption, queue size: \" + queue.size());\n        } else if (queue.size() < 100) {\n            // Resume when space available\n            consumer.resume(consumer.assignment());\n            log.info(\"Resumed consumption, queue size: \" + queue.size());\n        }\n\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n        for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n            queue.offer(record);\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Benefits:**\n- Prevents memory overflow\n- Smooth processing rate\n- Handles slow downstream systems\n\n### Error Recovery Best Practices\n\n```java\nprivate static final int MAX_RETRIES = 3;\nprivate static final Duration RETRY_BACKOFF = Duration.ofSeconds(1);\n\nwhile (true) {\n    try {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n        for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n            processRecord(record);\n        }\n        consumer.commitSync();\n    } catch (CommitFailedException e) {\n        // Fatal: consumer out of group\n        log.error(\"Consumer fenced or partitions lost, exiting\", e);\n        break;\n    } catch (RebalanceInProgressException e) {\n        // Transient: wait for rebalance\n        log.info(\"Rebalance in progress, retrying after delay\");\n        Thread.sleep(RETRY_BACKOFF.toMillis());\n        // Retry on next loop iteration\n    } catch (AuthorizationException | AuthenticationException e) {\n        // Configuration error: must fix and restart\n        log.error(\"Auth error, exiting\", e);\n        break;\n    } catch (TimeoutException e) {\n        // Transient: may retry\n        log.warn(\"Timeout during commit, may reprocess\", e);\n        // Retry on next loop iteration\n    } catch (WakeupException e) {\n        // Shutdown signal\n        log.info(\"Wakeup received, shutting down\");\n        break;\n    } catch (Exception e) {\n        // Other recoverable errors\n        log.error(\"Unexpected error, retrying\", e);\n        Thread.sleep(RETRY_BACKOFF.toMillis());\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Summary Table of Key Methods\n\n| Category | Method | Returns | Key Behavior |\n|----------|--------|---------|--------------|\n| **Subscription** | `subscribe(Collection)` | void | Subscribe to topics, enable rebalancing |\n| | `subscribe(Pattern)` | void | Subscribe to offset by timestamp |\n| **Metadata** | `partitionsFor(String)` | List | Get partition info for topic |\n| | `listTopics()` | Map | Get all topics in cluster |\n| **Lifecycle** | `close()` | void |
